					(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMoreShips 
					) 
				) 
			) 
		) 
		(ifthenelse 	(or 	(and 	(numPlanetsLessThan 	(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMoreShips 
						) 
						(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithLessPlanets 
						) 
					) 
					(numFleetsGreaterThan 	(totalOfFleetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithLessPlanets 
						) 
						(totalOfFleetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMorePlanets 
						) 
					) 
				) 
				(numFleetsEquals 	(totalOfFleetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMoreShips 
					) 
					(totalOfFleetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMoreFleets 
					) 
				) 
			) 
			(ifthenelse 	(numFleetsGreaterThan 	(totalOfFleetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMoreShips 
					) 
					(totalOfFleetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMorePlanets 
					) 
				) 
				(ifthenelse 	(numPlanetsEquals 	(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	myId 
						) 
						(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	myId 
						) 
					) 
					(issueOrderToNearestPercentageOfOrigin 	mySlowestGrowing 
						neutral 
						porcentaje050 
					) 
					(overwhelm 	myFastestGrowing 
						(slowestGrowing 	enemy 
						) 
					) 
				) 
				(ifthenelse 	(numShipEquals 	(totalOfShipsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithLessPlanets 
						) 
						(totalOfShipsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithLessPlanets 
						) 
					) 
					(overwhelm 	myStrongest 
						(slowestGrowing 	(ownedBy 	playerIdWithMoreFleets 
							) 
						) 
					) 
					(overwhelm 	myFastestGrowing 
						(fastestGrowing 	(ownedBy 	playerIdWithMoreFleets 
							) 
						) 
					) 
				) 
			) 
			(ifthenelse 	(numPlanetsEquals 	(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	myId 
					) 
					(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMorePlanets 
					) 
				) 
				(ifthenelse 	(numFleetsLessThan 	(totalOfFleetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMoreShips 
						) 
						(totalOfFleetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMorePlanets 
						) 
					) 
					(overwhelm 	myWeakest 
						(weakest 	enemy 
						) 
					) 
					(ifthenelse 	(playerIDEquals 	playerIdWithMoreFleets 
							playerIdWithMorePlanets 
						) 
						noOrder 
						(overwhelm 	myStrongest 
							(fastestGrowing 	enemy 
							) 
						) 
					) 
				) 
				(ifthenelse 	(and 	(numShipGreaterThan 	(totalOfShipsFromPlayer 	myId 
							) 
							(totalOfShipsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithLessFleets 
							) 
						) 
						(playerIDEquals 	playerIdWithLessShips 
							playerIdWithLessFleets 
						) 
					) 
					(overwhelm 	myWeakest 
						(weakest 	(ownedBy 	playerIdWithLessShips 
							) 
						) 
					) 
					(issueOrderToNearestPercentageOfOrigin 	myStrongest 
						neutral 
						porcentaje070 
					) 
				) 
			) 
		) 
		(ifthenelse 	(not 	(not 	(or 	(numPlanetsEquals 	(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMoreFleets 
							) 
							(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMoreShips 
							) 
						) 
						(numPlanetsGreaterThan 	(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithLessShips 
							) 
							(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithLessFleets 
							) 
						) 
					) 
				) 
			) 
			(ifthenelse 	(numShipEquals 	(totalOfShipsFromPlayer 	myId 
					) 
					(totalOfShipsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMorePlanets 
					) 
				) 
				(ifthenelse 	(numShipEquals 	(totalOfShipsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMorePlanets 
						) 
						(totalOfShipsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithLessFleets 
						) 
					) 
					(issueOrderPercentageOfOrigin 	myFastestGrowing 
						(fastestGrowing 	enemy 
						) 
						porcentaje005 
					) 
					(issueOrderToNearestPercentageOfOrigin 	myFastestGrowing 
						enemy 
						porcentaje070 
					) 
				) 
				(ifthenelse 	(numPlanetsGreaterThan 	(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMorePlanets 
						) 
						(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMoreShips 
						) 
					) 
					(issueOrderPercentageOfOrigin 	myStrongest 
						(weakest 	neutral 
						) 
						porcentaje050 
					) 
					(issueOrderPercentageOfOrigin 	myStrongest

					) 
				) 
			) 
			(ifthenelse 	(not 	(playerIDEquals 	playerIdWithMoreFleets 
						playerIdWithMoreShips 
					) 
				) 
				(ifthenelse 	(numShipEquals 	(totalOfShipsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithLessShips 
						) 
						(totalOfShipsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMorePlanets 
						) 
					) 
					(issueOrderPercentageOfOrigin 	mySlowestGrowing 
						(slowestGrowing 	enemy 
						) 
						porcentaje005 
					)

							playerIdWithLessPlanets 
						) 
						(issueOrderToNearestPercentageOfDestination 	mySlowestGrowing 
							enemy 
							porcentaje005 
						) 
						(issueOrderToNearestPercentageOfOrigin 	myWeakest 
							neutral 
							porcentaje090 
						) 
					)

				(ifthenelse 	(numPlanetsGreaterThan 	(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithLessShips 
						) 
						(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMoreFleets 
						) 
					) 
					(ifthenelse 	(numPlanetsEquals 	(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMoreFleets 
							) 
							(totalOfPlanetsFromPlayer 	playerIdWithMoreShips
